 somvaar kii raat 69 varshon main pehali baar chand, dharti ke sabase kareeb he
 This phenomenon is colloquially called a 'supermoon'
 is avadhi main yah apane aakaar se 14 pratishat bada or 30 pratishat zyada chamkila dikhaai degaa
 Earlier this view was seen by people in 1948
 ab iske 18 saal baad 25 november 2034 ko is vilakshan khagoleey ghatana kaa najaara dekhne ko milegaa

 uttari america samet duniya ke kai deshon main somvaar ke tadake hi yah najaara dekhne ko mila jabaki bharat main somvaar raat ko yah najaara dekh paanaa sambhav he

 kal tak masood ko pulavama hamale main clichit de rahe kuraishi ne ab kaha he ki wo bharat kii ore se die gaye dogier par gaur farmaayenge
 However, it is also considered to be Pakistan's move against terrorists by air strike
 saath hi ise samay kaatane kii waisi hi ranneeti mana ja rahaa he jaisi ranneeti mumbai ke 26-11 hamale ke baad pakistan ne apanaai thi
 The ISI uses terrorists fleeing into Pakistan to carry out attacks on India
 aise main unke khilaaf kisi bhi tarah kii karrwai ko dikhaava hi qaraar diya ja saktaa he
 Pakistan is so concerned about the safety of Masood Azhar that his ministers do not delay to deny the news of his death
 haalanki, pulavama hamale ke baad bhartiya vayusena kii karrwai ke saath-saath antarrashtriya manch par pakistan kii gheraabandi kaa ek or asar bhi dekha ja rahaa he
 On Monday, Pakistan passed a law under which UN sanctions would be enforced against those terrorists and their organizations
 pakistan ko ye kadam apni jameen par pal rahe aatankiyon par nakel kasne ko lekar vaishvik samudaay ke dabaav ke chalate uthaanaa padaa he
 Along with this it has been claimed by a big source of Pakistan government that the Pakistan government has decided to take strict action against terrorist organizations including jaish-e-mohammed's leader Masood Azhar
 pakistani adhikari kii maane to ye kadam bharat ke saath bade tanaav ko kam karne ke liye uthaaya ja rahaa he
 It is being told that this step can be taken at any time
 samaajawaadee party ke mukhiya mulaayam singh yadav mangalvaar ko 77 saal ke ho gaye
 Mulayam, who had been struggling with his clan sometime back, has seen all the ups and downs in his political career
 isi maheene unki party ne 25 saal puure kiye hai
 Samajwadi Party Travel News On October, 1992, Mulayam Singh Yadav announced to form a Samajwadi Party at Begum Hazrat Mahal Park, Lucknow
 ram manohar lohia or raaj narayan jaise samaajawaadee vichaardhaara ke netaaon kii chhatrachhaaya main raajnneeti kaa kakehara seekhney vaale mulaayam vaise to sapa ke gathan se pehle hi uttar pradesh ke siem ban chuke the
 But he had no party of his own
 1980 ke aakhir main wo uttar pradesh main lok dal ke adhyaksh bane the jo baad main janata dal kaa hissaa ban gaya
 The Samajwadi Party story continued along the political journey of Mulayam Singh
 mulaayam 1989 main pehali baar uttar pradesh ke siem bane
 In November 1990, when VP Singh's government fell at the Center, Mulayam Singh joined Chandra Shekhar's Janata Dal (samajwadi)
 or congress ke samarthan se siem kii kursi par virajman rahe
 When the Congress withdrew support in April 1991, Mulayam Singh's government fell
 1991 main upi main madhyavadhi chunaav hue jisamen mulaayam singh kii party haar gai or bijepi soobe main satta main ai
 The next year, in 1992, when Mulayam Singh Yadav raised his party, he did not have a big support base
 november 1993 main upi main vidhansabha ke chunaav hone the
 The SP chief tied up with the Bahujan Samaj Party to prevent the BJP from coming back to power
 samaajawaadee party kaa yah apana pehla bada prayog tha
 This experiment of Mulayam was also successful in the political atmosphere born after the Babri Masjid demolition
 congress or janata dal ke samarthan se mulaayam singh phir satta main aae or siem bane
 At that time, the demand for separate Uttarakhand was gaining momentum
 2 oktober 1994 ko alag uttarakhand kii maang kar rahe logon par mujffarnagar main firing hui
 This incident is known as Rampur Tiraha firing incident
 aarope laga ki tatkaaleen siem mulaayam singh ke nirdesh par pulisavaalon ne firing kii jisamen 6 log maare gaye
 On June 2, 1995, Mulayam was ousted from power the next day due to misbehavior with Mayawati in the state guest house scandal in Lucknow
 samaajawaadee party kii saakh par bhi isse bada batta laga
 After exiting the politics of the state, Mulayam was now focused on the politics of the center
 mulaayam ko laga ki ab samaajawaadee party ko rashtriya str par pahchaan dilaani he
 Mulayam contested the Lok Sabha elections from Mainpuri seat in 1996 and also won
 centre main sanyukt morche kii sarkaar bani or sapa is gathjod kaa hissaa
 SP chief Mulayam Singh's name was being fixed for the Prime Minister
 mulaayam devgauda sarkaar main raksha mantri bane
 He also held this position in the Gujral government
 haalanki 1998 main yah sarkaar gir gai or desh main phir se aam chunaav hue
 But Mulayam knew that the existence of the Samajwadi Party would continue in its victory in UP
 isliye unhone soobe main phir se sanghathan ko khadaa karnaa shuru kiya or 2003 ke vidhansabha chunaav main samaajawaadee party ko jeet naseeb hui
 On 29 August 2003, Mulayam Singh Yadav was sworn in as the Chief Minister of the state again
 soobe main chaar saal tak samaajawaadee party kii sarkaar rahi
 However, the 2004 Lok Sabha election was also historic for the Samajwadi Party
 party ko 35 siten hasil huin
 But Delhi could not get a share of power
 iske baad ke paanch saal samaajawaadee party ke liye behad uthal-puthal bhare rahe
 The urge for national politics on the one hand, the longing to remain a regional satraps
 is duvidha main party kaa bantaadhaar hone laga
 The workers were also beginning to go on unbridled
 2009 ke loksabhaa chunaav main samaajawaadee party ko mahaj 22 siten milin
 Mulayam then took a big decision
 rajya vidhansabha main netaa vipaksh kii kursi par chote bhai shivpal yadav ko bitha diya or khud dilli kii siyasat kii kaman sambhaal lee
 During this period Azam Khan, the big Muslim face of the party, left the SP
 rajbabbar or benny prasad verma jaise netaaon ne bhi samaajawaadee party kaa saath chhod diya or party main amar singh kaa varchasv badhata gaya
 Kalyan Singh, one of the accused in the Babri demolition scandal, was inducted into the Samajwadi Party who felt neglected in the BJP
 kalyaan singh ke samaajawaadee party main aane se mulaayam ke kai saathiyon ne party chhod di jo netaji ke siyaasi safar main kadam se kadam milakar chale the
 Veteran socialist leaders like Janeshwar Mishra, Ramsharan Das and Laxmikant Verma died
 2007 ke vidhansabha chunaav main prachand bahumat se satta main ai bahujan samaaj party ke aakraamak taur tareekon ne samaajawaadee party ko kamjor karne main ahm bhoomika nibhaai
 But Mulayam Singh, who was away in power for five years, was not going to give up so soon
 2012 ke chunaav se pehle netaji ne apane bete akhilesh yadav ko uttar pradesh sapa kii kaman saunpi
 Amar Singh was also dropped from the party in February 2010
 ajam kii ghar vaapasi hui to kalyaan se sapa kaa peechha chuta
 Akhilesh worked hard before the election
 akhilesh kya, puraa samaajawaadee kunba sadakon par utarkar netaji ke sapanom ko puraa karne main jute gaya
 The result was also seen when the 2012 Assembly elections brought unexpected results in favor of SP
 akhilesh soobe ke siem bane or samaajawaadee party main duusari peedi ne dastak di
 Gradually, the number of Yadav family members in the party also increased
 aaj kii taarikh main is parivaar ke 20 sadsy samaajawaadee party kaa hissaa hai
 This phase of Samajwadi Party is completely different from the earlier period
 akhilesh ke kaam karne kaa tarika netaji se bilkul juda he
 For four-and-a-half years, everything went well within the party and the government, but as soon as the next assembly was called, discord started in the country's largest political house
 chah saal tak party se dur rahe amar singh kii ghar vaapasi hui
 He was made the General Secretary and sent to Rajya Sabha
 benny prasad verma kii bhi ghar vaapasi hui or rajyasabha bheje gaye
 Akhilesh opposed the merger of Bahubali Mukhtar Ansari's party with the Samajwadi Party with the support of Chacha Shivpal and Amar Singh
 lekin netaji ke aage akhilesh kii nahin chali
 Then CM Akhilesh showed the way out of his cabinet to some ministers accused of corruption
 akhilesh ne apni cabinet main ahm mantralayon kaa jimmaa sambhaal rahe chachaa shivpal yadav kii bhi cabinet se chuttee kar di
 Mulayam Singh tried to balance, took away the post of state president from his son and handed it over to his brother
 haalanki baad main shivpal kii cabinet main bhi vaapasi ho gai or kalah kaa yah daur shant hua
 But Akhilesh could not get the post of state president back
 phir akhilesh ne chachaa shivpal samet kuch mantriyon kii apane cabinet se chuttee kar di
 Another round of discord began in the Yadav family
 mulaayam ke chachere bhai or rajyasabha sadsy ramgopal yadav party se nikaal die gaye
 a few more close friends of Akhilesh were also discharged from the party
 lekin is baar akhilesh jhuke nahin
 Even after millions of efforts, uncle has not returned to Shivpal's government
 taaja kalah ke dauraan kai baar to aisa laga ki party hi tut jaaegi
 But Netaji has handled everything
 ab akhilesh agle chunaav kii taiyaariyon main jute gaye hai to shivpal ko chunaav purv prastaavit mahagathbandhan ke liye dusron dalon ko saath laane kii jimmedaari netaji ne saunp di he
 In such a situation, the 2017 assembly election is going to write a new chapter in the history of Samajwadi Party

 ve kehete hai, ''iskaa andhadhundh istemaal nahin hona chahie, balki iskaa istemaal bharat kii samprabhutaa or suraksha, baahar ke deshon ke saath dostana rishton or saarvajanik vyavastha ke hit main anuchhed 19(2) ke praavdhaanon ke mutabik hi hona chahie
